<div id="review_1215007521" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1215007521" />
    <a title="Lisazj1" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5816343-lisazj1"><img alt="Lisazj1" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1337769434p2/5816343.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1215007521?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisazj1" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisazj1" href="/user/show/5816343-lisazj1">Lisazj1</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=audible">audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=friends-and-family">friends-and-family</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=law-enforcement-pi">law-enforcement-pi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=characters-i-wish-would-diaf">characters-i-wish-would-diaf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=crime-mystery-thriller">crime-mystery-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5816343-lisazj1?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1215007521" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14614352935314994441">4.5 stars. An entrancing read/listen. Beautifully written, absolutely compelling story. Even when it was a little heavy on the melodrama, I could not stop listening. I spent lots of extra time in my car listening, after I'd arrived wherever I was driving to! The reader, Jill Tanner, was fabulous, immersing me in the sounds, sights and life of London's Whitechapel district. The story has the most amazing, rich period atmosphere, it was so easy to get lost in it.<br/><br/>Lots of wonderful characters, most </span>
  <span id="freeText14614352935314994441" style="display:none">4.5 stars. An entrancing read/listen. Beautifully written, absolutely compelling story. Even when it was a little heavy on the melodrama, I could not stop listening. I spent lots of extra time in my car listening, after I'd arrived wherever I was driving to! The reader, Jill Tanner, was fabulous, immersing me in the sounds, sights and life of London's Whitechapel district. The story has the most amazing, rich period atmosphere, it was so easy to get lost in it.<br /><br />Lots of wonderful characters, most of all Fiona Finnegan <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[, who the author made me love even while not minding that she was a complete and total Mary Sue, which is quite a feat as far as I'm concerned <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Jennifer Donnelly did an outstanding job of taking me into Fiona's life and all that she experiences and accomplishes, despite however the odds were against her. She was a determined, 18 year old girl from one of the poorest parts of London, with almost no money but lots of dreams and plans and she was an absolute badass who did not know how to give up. I loved it.<br /><br />The one real aggravation I had that kept me from giving this 5 stars was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ how bloody stupid Fiona began behaving once Burton was on the loose after trying to kill her in front of all those witnesses. The man was obviously unhinged, she'd taken literally everything from him and he had nothing to lose by staying to finish her off. He killed her Da over a penny per hour raise and she took his whole life. Then brilliant, intelligent, canny Fiona decides to traipse all over London unescorted and listens to <i>no one</i>, apparently smothers that great intuition that kept her alive so many times before and walks into a set up from a TYPEWRITTEN note from Joe, *which caused her wharf manager and bodyguard to be murdered by Burton* and I was just...."who is the bleedin' idiot who replaced Fiona?" O.O *I ranted all this in Roddy O'Mara's voice, LOL* Perfect example of what I meant by unnecessary melodrama.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Still, all that said, I loved everything and everyone else, and was happy with how the story ended. I'll most definitely be reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/396266.The_Winter_Rose__The_Tea_Rose___2_" title="The Winter Rose (The Tea Rose, #2) by Jennifer Donnelly" rel="nofollow noopener">The Winter Rose</a>. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14614352935314994441" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_147743007" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/147743007" />
    <a title="Eileen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3650310-eileen"><img alt="Eileen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1322429351p2/3650310.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/147743007?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eileen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eileen" href="/user/show/3650310-eileen">Eileen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780007155569" href="/book/show/1062560.The_Tea_Rose">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3650310-eileen?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3650310-eileen?shelf=read-2011">read-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3650310-eileen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3650310-eileen?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3650310-eileen?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer147743007" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17168608343348523476">I drink a lot of tea, roses are one of my favorite flowers and I love historical fiction and that's the reason why I put this book on my to-read-list. It didn't disappoint me at all! It sucked me in from the beginning until the very exciting end. Unfortunately I was busy at work, because otherwise I wouldn't have been able to put the book down. This book needs a cold winters day, a comfortable couch, a big bar of chocolate and hot tea.......... You'll have an incredible read!<br/><br/>The story is about r</span>
  <span id="freeText17168608343348523476" style="display:none">I drink a lot of tea, roses are one of my favorite flowers and I love historical fiction and that's the reason why I put this book on my to-read-list. It didn't disappoint me at all! It sucked me in from the beginning until the very exciting end. Unfortunately I was busy at work, because otherwise I wouldn't have been able to put the book down. This book needs a cold winters day, a comfortable couch, a big bar of chocolate and hot tea.......... You'll have an incredible read!<br /><br />The story is about revenge, love, willpower, deception and is very captivating. The characters felt to me like real people. Fee is so incredibly strong and it's great to see how she matures trough the story. My favorite character by far is Nicholas Soames. Yes, he's a spoiled brat, but he had a really difficult life and I read his life story with tears in my eyes. I absolutely felt an emotional connection with him and I would love to have him as my friend. I will not forget him any time soon! <br /><br />My favorite quote is: <br />"I've always admired your rather formidable will, your refusal to back away from difficulties, but sometimes strength isn't about perseverance. Sometimes it's about knowing when to quit."<br />I'm talking from my personal experience when I say that this quote is very very true! When you are a fighter the hardest thing is(to know when)to stop, because it's the wisest thing to do and we shouldn't see it as defeat.<br /><br />I hope the two sequels are as good as this one. I'm definitely going to read them.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17168608343348523476" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1073691617" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1073691617" />
    <a title="Natasa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3742075-natasa"><img alt="Natasa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1533387613p2/3742075.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1073691617?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasa" href="/user/show/3742075-natasa">Natasa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3742075-natasa?shelf=new-york">new-york</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3742075-natasa?shelf=victorian-era">victorian-era</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1073691617" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7981202728047256091">The first section of this book was great. Ms. Donnelly captured the feel of lower-class, Victorian London during the time of Jack the Ripper, and her characters were exciting, fully realized human beings, not just fictional standbys. The second part of “The Tea Rose” was heartbreaking to me because the first part opened so strongly. I skimmed halfway through the second part, unable to sustain interest, and only finished the book with half-hearted interest.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('51JfgpuWYmsBG/JB3MtuVNfe4IvcNtlecOUp1bGE74PddDZQIMirA6YwRiArPmSLAYEHQxK7Vzkrm29kfMcdGQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GJ7HQazFhDKQ4PeTkWT/4k26l6Wi62b9j7uzD8+6SXYiuK6TF5tNWjfLQ/JmkfU9m+VwbWxm6JrUxfW+Avm77A==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11824778737884036139">Jennifer Donnelly is the author of thirteen novels - <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/poisoned/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Poisoned</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/stepsister/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Stepsister</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/lostinabook/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lost in a Book</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/theseshallowgraves/' rel='nofollow noopener'>These Shallow Graves</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/sea-spell/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sea Spell</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/dark-tide/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Dark Tide</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/rogue-wave/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rogue Wave</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/deep-blue/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Deep Blue</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/revolution/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Revolution</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/a-northern-light/' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Northern Light</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/the-tea-rose/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Tea Rose</a>, <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/the-winter-rose/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Winter Rose</a> and <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/the-wild-rose/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Wild Rose</a> - and <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/humble-pie/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Humble Pie</a>, a picture book for children. She is a co-author of <a href='https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/fatal-throne/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fatal Throne</a>, which explores the lives of King Henry VIII's six wives, for which she wrote the </span>
  <span id="freeText11824778737884036139" style="display:none">Jennifer Donnelly is the author of thirteen novels - <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/poisoned/" rel="nofollow noopener">Poisoned</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/stepsister/" rel="nofollow noopener">Stepsister</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/lostinabook/" rel="nofollow noopener">Lost in a Book</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/theseshallowgraves/" rel="nofollow noopener">These Shallow Graves</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/sea-spell/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sea Spell</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/dark-tide/" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Tide</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/rogue-wave/" rel="nofollow noopener">Rogue Wave</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/deep-blue/" rel="nofollow noopener">Deep Blue</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/revolution/" rel="nofollow noopener">Revolution</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/a-northern-light/" rel="nofollow noopener">A Northern Light</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/the-tea-rose/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Tea Rose</a>, <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/the-winter-rose/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Winter Rose</a> and <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/the-wild-rose/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wild Rose</a> - and <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/humble-pie/" rel="nofollow noopener">Humble Pie</a>, a picture book for children. She is a co-author of <a href="https://www.jenniferdonnelly.com/book/fatal-throne/" rel="nofollow noopener">Fatal Throne</a>, which explores the lives of King Henry VIII's six wives, for which she wrote the part of Anna of Cleves, Henry's fourth wife.<br /><br />She grew up in New York State, in Lewis and Westchester counties, and attended the University of Rochester where she majored in English Literature and European History. <br /><br />Jennifer’s first novel, The Tea Rose, an epic historical novel set in London and New York in the late 19th century, was called “exquisite” by Booklist, “so much fun” by the Washington Post, a “guilty pleasure” by People and was named a Top Pick by the Romantic Times. The Rose trilogy continued with The Winter Rose and The Wild Rose.<br /><br />Her second novel, A Northern Light, set in the Adirondacks of 1906, against the backdrop of an infamous murder, won the Carnegie Medal, the Los Angeles Times Book Prize, the Borders Original Voices Award, and was named a Printz Honor book. Described as “rich and true” by The New York Times, the book was named to the Best Book lists of The Times (London), The Irish Times, The Financial Times, Publishers Weekly, Booklist and the School Library Journal. In 2015, TIME Magazine named it one of the 100 best young adult books of all time.<br /><br />Revolution was named a Best Book by Amazon, Kirkus, School Library Journal, and the Chicago Public Library, and was nominated for a Carnegie Medal. The audio edition was awarded an Odyssey Honor for Excellence.<br /><br />In 2014, Jennifer teamed up with Disney to launch the bestselling Waterfire Saga, an epic series about six mermaids on a quest to rid the world of an ancient evil. The first book in the series, Deep Blue, was released in May, 2014; the second, Rogue Wave, launched in January 2015; the third, Dark Tide, came out in October 2015; and the fourth, Sea Spell, is scheduled for release in June 2016.<br /><br />In November 2015, Jennifer released the historical novel These Shallow Graves, which received starred reviews from Booklist, Publishers Weekly and Shelf Awareness, and was named a Junior Library Guild Selection. <br /><br />Jennifer worked with Disney again in 2017, when she published Beauty and the Beast: Lost in a Book, an original story to accompany the blockbuster Beauty and the Beast film. Lost in a Book expands on the classic tale, exploring the growing friendship between Belle and the Beast as well as Belle's ordeal within the pages of Nevermore, a magical book from which she narrowly escapes. <br /><br />Jennifer returned to historical fiction with Fatal Throne, a book about Henry VIII and his six wives published by Random House/Schwartz &amp; Wade in 2018. For this project, Jennifer joined six other authors (Candace Fleming, M.T. Anderson, Stephanie Hemphill, Deborah Hopkinson, Linda Sue Park, and </span>
  <a data-text-id="11824778737884036139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
